| {\x0D
| case '@':\x0D
| result+='\@';break;\x0D
| case "'":\x0D
| result+="\'";break;\x0D
| case '"':\x0D
| result+='\"';break;\x0D
| case '^':\x0D
| result+='\^';break;\x0D
| case '[':\x0D
| result+='\[';break;\x0D
| case ']':\x0D
| result+='\]';break;\x0D
| case '#':\x0D
| result+='%23';break;\x0D
| case '%':\x0D
| result+='%25';break;\x0D
| case '&':\x0D
| result+='%26';break;\x0D
| case '+':\x0D
| result+='%2B';break;\x0D
| default:\x0D
| result+=ch;break;\x0D
| }\x0D
| }\x0D
| return result;\x0D
| }\x0D
| function trimInnerSpaces(i_Cntrl)\x0D

| if(typeof(i_Cntrl) == "string")\x0D
| cntrl = document.getElementById(i_Cntrl);\x0D
| cntrl.value= cntrl.value.trim(false,true);\x0D
| }\x0D
| function GetPublicKey()\x0D

| return (rsaPublicKey=='') ? 'none' : rsaPublicKey;\x0D
| }\x0D
| else\x0D
| return 'disabled';\x0D
| }\x0D

| function SendLoginXML()\x0D
| {\x0D
| var publicKey = GetPublicKey();\x0D
| if (publicKey!='none' && publicKey !='disabled')\x0D
| {\x0D
| var startStr="-----BEGIN RSA PUBLIC KEY-----";\x0D
| var endStr="-----END RSA PUBLIC KEY-----";\x0D
| publicKey=publicKey.substring(publicKey.indexOf(startStr)+startStr.length,publicKey.indexOf(endStr))\x0D
| }\x0D
| else if (publicKey=='none')\x0D
| {\x0D
| DisplayLoginError("12");\x0D
| return;\x0D
| }\x0D
| document.getElementById("lblProg").style.display = "";\x0D
| document.getElementById("dvLoginErr").style.display = "none";\x0D
| document.getElementById("tblLogoutMsg").style.display = "none";\x0D
| var UserCntrl = document.getElementById("userName$query");\x0D
| var passwCntrl = document.getElementById("password");\x0D
| trimInnerSpaces(UserCntrl);\x0D
| trimInnerSpaces(passwCntrl);\x0D
| var user= createQueryUserName(UserCntrl.value);\x0D
| var passw=createQueryUserName(passwCntrl.value);\x0D
| if (publicKey =='disabled') {\x0D
| var newPath = './System.xml?action=login&user='+user+'&password=' + passw+"&ssd=true&";\x0D
| }\x0D
| else {\x0D
| var rsa = new RSAKey();\x0D
| convertPublicKey(publicKey)\x0D
| rsa.setPublic(n,e);\x0D
| var str ='user='+user+'&password=' + passw+'&ssd=true&';\x0D
| var res = rsa.encrypt(str);\x0D
| var newPath = './System.xml?action=login&cred='+res;\x0D
| }\x0D
| homeShowProg(true, null, 10);\x0D
| xmlhttp=null;\x0D
| if (window.XMLHttpRequest) {\x0D
| xmlhttp=new XMLHttpRequest();\x0D
| }\x0D
| else if (window.ActiveXObject) {\x0D
| xmlhttp=new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");\x0D
| }\x0D
| if (xmlhttp!=null) {\x0D
| loginProcFinish = 0;\x0D
| loginProcCounter = 20;\x0D
| checkLoginProc();\x0D
| xmlhttp.onreadystatechange=state_Change;\x0D
| xmlhttp.open("GET",newPath,true);\x0D
| xmlhttp.send(null);\x0D
| }\x0D
| else {\x0D
| DisplayLoginError("6")\x0D
| }\x0D
| }\x0D

| e=resultArr[2].substring(0,resultArr[2].indexOf(":")).trim();\x0D

| function get_tagValue(XMLstr,tagName)\x0D
| {\x0D
| var ret='';\x0D
| var pos=XMLstr.indexOf("<"+tagName+">");\x0D
| if (pos>0){\x0D
| var pos1=XMLstr.indexOf(">",pos);\x0D
| if (pos1>=0){\x0D
| var pos2=XMLstr.indexOf("<",pos1);\x0D
| ret = XMLstr.substr(pos1+1,pos2-pos1-1);\x0D
| }\x0D
| }\x0D
| return ret;\x0D
| }\x0D

| function DisplayLogoutMess(messCode)\x0D
| {\x0D
| var logoutMess;\x0D
| var moduleType;\x0D
| for(var i=1; formele["rlPhdModuleType$repeat?"+i]; i++)\x0D
| {\x0D
| if(formele["rlPhdModuleRole$repeat?"+i].value <= 2)\x0D
| moduleType=formele["rlPhdModuleType$repeat?"+i].value;\x0D
| }\x0D
| switch (messCode)\x0D
| {\x0D
| case "Manual":\x0D
| if ((parseInt(moduleType,10) < 52) || (parseInt(moduleType,10) > 57))\x0D
| logoutMess="4";\x0D
| else\x0D
| logoutMess="22";\x0D
| break;\x0D
| case "TimeOut":\x0D
| logoutMess="5";\x0D
| break;\x0D
| case "Response":\x0D
| logoutMess="6";\x0D
| break;\x0D
| }\x0D
| if (logoutMess!=null)\x0D
| {\x0D
| pgTkn.setTokenWithError("cellMessage",logoutMess);\x0D
| document.getElementById("tblLogoutMsg").style.display = "";\x0D
| }\x0D
| }\x0D

| function ResourceHandler(src, id)\x0D
| {\x0D
| this.status = 0;\x0D
| var resourceNode = document.getElementById(id);\x0D
| var that = this;\x0D
| this.load = function()\x0D
| {\x0D
| this.status = 1;\x0D
| resourceNode.onload = function(){that.status = 2};\x0D
| resourceNode.onerror = function(){that.status = -1};\x0D
| resourceNode.onabort = function(){that.status = -1};\x0D
| resourceNode.src = src;\x0D
| setTimeout(timer, 3000);\x0D
| }\x0D
| function timer()\x0D
| {\x0D
| if (that.status == 1)\x0D
| resourceNode.src = "";\x0D
| }\x0D
| }\x0D
| function ResourceCollection(callback)\x0D
| {\x0D
| var intervalId = 0;\x0D
| var that = this;\x0D
| this.resourceHandlerArr = [];\x0D
| if (typeof callback != "function")\x0D
| callback = function(){};\x0D
| this.startLoad = function()\x0D
| {\x0D
| for (var i = 0; i < Math.min(this.queuesNumber, this.resourceHandlerArr.length); i ++)\x0D
| loader();\x0D
| if (this.queuesNumber && this.resourceHandlerArr.length)\x0D
| intervalId = setInterval(loader, 20);\x0D
| }\x0D
| function loader()\x0D
| {\x0D
| var status;\x0D
| var loadingCount = 0;\x0D
| var finishedCount = 0;\x0D
| var idxToLoad = -1;\x0D
| for (var i = 0; i < that.resourceHandlerArr.length; i ++)\x0D
| {\x0D
| status = that.resourceHandlerArr[i].status;\x0D
| if (status == 0)\x0D
| {\x0D
| idxToLoad = i;\x0D
| break;\x0D
| }\x0D
| else if (status == 1)\x0D
| loadingCount ++;\x0D
| else\x0D
| finishedCount ++;\x0D
| }\x0D
| if (finishedCount == that.resourceHandlerArr.length)\x0D
| {\x0D
| clearInterval(intervalId);\x0D
| callback();\x0D
| return;\x0D
| }\x0D
| if (loadingCount >= that.queuesNumber)\x0D
| return;\x0D
| if (idxToLoad == -1)\x0D
| return;\x0D
| else\x0D
| that.resourceHandlerArr[idxToLoad].load();\x0D
| }\x0D
| }\x0D
| ResourceCollection.prototype.queuesNumber = 2;\x0D
| ResourceCollection.prototype.addResourceHandler = function(src, id)\x0D
| {\x0D
| this.resourceHandlerArr.push(new ResourceHandler(src, id));\x0D
| }\x0D

| {\x0D

| $("barPageTop").style.backgroundImage = "url(../images/ciscoImages/bar.gif)";\x0D
| $("barPageBottom").style.backgroundImage = "url(../images/ciscoImages/bar.gif)";\x0D
| $("barContextTop").style.backgroundImage = "url(../images/ciscoImages/bar.gif)";\x0D
| $("barContextBottom").style.backgroundImage = "url(../images/ciscoImages/bar.gif)";\x0D
| $("topLeftPage").style.backgroundImage = "url(../images/ciscoImages/topLeft.gif)";\x0D
| $("topLeftContext").style.backgroundImage = "url(../images/ciscoImages/topLeft.gif)";\x0D
| $("topRightPage").style.backgroundImage = "url(../images/ciscoImages/topRight.gif)";\x0D
| $("topRightContext").style.backgroundImage = "url(../images/ciscoImages/topRight.gif)";\x0D
| $("bottomLeftPage").style.backgroundImage = "url(../images/ciscoImages/bottomLeft.gif)";\x0D
| $("bottomLeftContext").style.backgroundImage = "url(../images/ciscoImages/bottomLeft.gif)";\x0D
| $("bottomRightPage").style.backgroundImage = "url(../images/ciscoImages/bottomRight.gif)";\x0D
| $("bottomRightContext").style.backgroundImage = "url(../images/ciscoImages/bottomRight.gif)";\x0D
| function $(id){return document.getElementById(id)}\x0D

| function PostLoad()\x0D
| {\x0D
| rc = new ResourceCollection(PostLoadCallback);\x0D
| var resArr = [\x0D
| ["../images/ciscoImages/logo_cis.gif", "imgLogo"],\x0D

| ];\x0D

| rc.startLoad();\x0D
| }\x0D

| function Octet2StrReturn(Octet)\x0D
| {\x0D
| var temp;\x0D
| var i=0;\x0D
| var str="";\x0D
| Octet=Octet.toUpperCase();\x0D
| while(i<Octet.length)\x0D
| {\x0D
| temp=Octet.slice(i,i+2);\x0D
| temp=Hex2Ascii(temp);\x0D
| temp=String.fromCharCode(temp);\x0D
| str=str.concat(temp);\x0D
| i+=2;\x0D
| }\x0D
| return str ;\x0D
| }\x0D
| function Hex2Ascii(input)\x0D
| {\x0D
| origin=16;\x0D
| dest=10;\x0D
| base="0123456789ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ";\x0D
| c=0; Result="";\x0D
| for (t=1; t<=input.length; t++)\x0D
| {\x0D
| if ( (input.substring(t-1,t)>='a') && (input.substring(t-1,t)<='z') )\x0D
| b=base.indexOf(input.substring(t-1,t).toUpperCase());\x0D
| else b=base.indexOf(input.substring(t-1,t));\x0D
| n=b*(Math.pow (origin, input.length-t));\x0D
| c+=n;\x0D
| }\x0D
| a=100;\x0D
| while (a>0 && c < Math.pow (dest, a)) { a--; }\x0D
| while (a>-1)\x0D
| {\x0D
| e=Math.pow (dest, a);\x0D
| a--;\x0D
| d=((c-(c%e))/e)+1;\x0D
| c=c%e; Ciffer=base.substring(d-1, d); Result = Result + Ciffer;\x0D
| }\x0D
| return Result;\x0D
| }\x0D
| function convertDnsMib2Octet(pOctetStr)\x0D
| {\x0D
| var i = 0;\x0D
| var curr_size = 0;\x0D
| var curr_octet = "";;\x0D
| var mib_value = "";\x0D
| while(i < pOctetStr.length-2)\x0D
| {\x0D
| if (i != 0)\x0D
| {\x0D
| mib_value = mib_value.concat(".");\x0D
| }\x0D
| curr_size = pOctetStr.slice(i, i + 2);\x0D
| curr_size = parseInt(curr_size,16);\x0D
| i += 2;\x0D
| curr_octet = pOctetStr.slice(i, i + curr_size * 2);\x0D
| i += curr_size * 2;\x0D
| mib_value += (Octet2StrReturn(curr_octet));\x0D
| }\x0D
| return mib_value;\x0D
| }\x0D
| function createQueryUserName(userName)\x0D
| {\x0D
| var result = "";\x0D
| for (var i=0;i<userName.length;i++)\x0D
| {\x0D
| var ch = userName.charAt(i);\x0D
| switch (ch)\x0D
| {\x0D
| case '@':\x0D
| result+='\@';break;\x0D
| case "'":\x0D
| result+="\'";break;\x0D
| case '"':\x0D
| result+='\"';break;\x0D
| case '^':\x0D
| result+='\^';break;\x0D
| case '[':\x0D
| result+='\[';break;\x0D
| case ']':\x0D
| result+='\]';break;\x0D
| case '#':\x0D
| result+='%23';break;\x0D
| case '%':\x0D
| result+='%25';break;\x0D
| case '&':\x0D
| result+='%26';break;\x0D
| case '+':\x0D
| result+='%2B';break;\x0D
| default:\x0D
| result+=ch;break;\x0D
| }\x0D
| }\x0D
| return result;\x0D
| }\x0D

| if (pos1>=0){\x0D
| var pos2=XMLstr.indexOf("<",pos1);\x0D
| ret = XMLstr.substr(pos1+1,pos2-pos1-1);\x0D
| }\x0D
| }\x0D
| return ret;\x0D

| function DisplayLogoutMess(messCode)\x0D
| {\x0D
| var logoutMess;\x0D
| var moduleType;\x0D
| for(var i=1; formele["rlPhdModuleType$repeat?"+i]; i++)\x0D
| {\x0D
| if(formele["rlPhdModuleRole$repeat?"+i].value <= 2)\x0D
| moduleType=formele["rlPhdModuleType$repeat?"+i].value;\x0D
| }\x0D
| switch (messCode)\x0D
| {\x0D
| case "Manual":\x0D
| if ((parseInt(moduleType,10) < 52) || (parseInt(moduleType,10) > 57))\x0D
| logoutMess="4";\x0D
| else\x0D
| logoutMess="22";\x0D
| break;\x0D
| case "TimeOut":\x0D
| logoutMess="5";\x0D
| break;\x0D
| case "Response":\x0D
| logoutMess="6";\x0D
| break;\x0D
| }\x0D

| {\x0D
| pgTkn.setTokenWithError("cellMessage",logoutMess);\x0D

| function ResourceHandler(src, id)\x0D
| {\x0D
| this.status = 0;\x0D
| var resourceNode = document.getElementById(id);\x0D
| var that = this;\x0D
| this.load = function()\x0D
| {\x0D
| this.status = 1;\x0D
| resourceNode.onload = function(){that.status = 2};\x0D
| resourceNode.onerror = function(){that.status = -1};\x0D
| resourceNode.onabort = function(){that.status = -1};\x0D
| resourceNode.src = src;\x0D
| setTimeout(timer, 3000);\x0D
| }\x0D
| function timer()\x0D
| {\x0D
| if (that.status == 1)\x0D
| resourceNode.src = "";\x0D
| }\x0D
| }\x0D
| function ResourceCollection(callback)\x0D
| {\x0D
| var intervalId = 0;\x0D
| var that = this;\x0D
| this.resourceHandlerArr = [];\x0D
| if (typeof callback != "function")\x0D
| callback = function(){};\x0D
| this.startLoad = function()\x0D
| {\x0D
| for (var i = 0; i < Math.min(this.queuesNumber, this.resourceHandlerArr.length); i ++)\x0D
| loader();\x0D
| if (this.queuesNumber && this.resourceHandlerArr.length)\x0D
| intervalId = setInterval(loader, 20);\x0D
| }\x0D
| function loader()\x0D
| {\x0D
| var status;\x0D
| var loadingCount = 0;\x0D
| var finishedCount = 0;\x0D
| var idxToLoad = -1;\x0D
| for (var i = 0; i < that.resourceHandlerArr.length; i ++)\x0D
| {\x0D
| status = that.resourceHandlerArr[i].status;\x0D
| if (status == 0)\x0D
| {\x0D
| idxToLoad = i;\x0D
| break;\x0D
| }\x0D
| else if (status == 1)\x0D
| loadingCount ++;\x0D
| else\x0D
| finishedCount ++;\x0D
| }\x0D
| if (finishedCount == that.resourceHandlerArr.length)\x0D
| {\x0D
| clearInterval(intervalId);\x0D
| callback();\x0D
| return;\x0D
| }\x0D
| if (loadingCount >= that.queuesNumber)\x0D
| return;\x0D
| if (idxToLoad == -1)\x0D
| return;\x0D
| else\x0D
| that.resourceHandlerArr[idxToLoad].load();\x0D
| }\x0D
| }\x0D
| ResourceCollection.prototype.queuesNumber = 2;\x0D
| ResourceCollection.prototype.addResourceHandler = function(src, id)\x0D
| {\x0D
| this.resourceHandlerArr.push(new ResourceHandler(src, id));\x0D
| }\x0D
| var PostLoadCallback = function()\x0D
| {\x0D
| DisplayTranslucentPNGInIE6_Login("imgInfo", "../kubrick/images/Status_information_icon.png");\x0D
| $("barPageTop").style.backgroundImage = "url(../images/ciscoImages/bar.gif)";\x0D
| $("barPageBottom").style.backgroundImage = "url(../images/ciscoImages/bar.gif)";\x0D
| $("barContextTop").style.backgroundImage = "url(../images/ciscoImages/bar.gif)";\x0D

| if(timeout)\x0D

| }\x0D

| {\x0D
| document.getElementById("dvProgVeil").style.display="none";\x0D
| document.getElementById("dvProgBar").style.display="none";\x0D

|   VULNERABLE:
|   SSL/TLS MITM vulnerability (CCS Injection)
|     State: VULNERABLE
|     Risk factor: High
|       OpenSSL before 0.9.8za, 1.0.0 before 1.0.0m, and 1.0.1 before 1.0.1h

|   Transport Layer Security (TLS) Protocol DHE_EXPORT Ciphers Downgrade MitM (Logjam)
|     State: VULNERABLE
|     IDs:  BID:74733  CVE:CVE-2015-4000
|       The Transport Layer Security (TLS) protocol contains a flaw that is
|       triggered when handling Diffie-Hellman key exchanges defined with
|       the DHE_EXPORT cipher. This may allow a man-in-the-middle attacker
|       to downgrade the security of a TLS session to 512-bit export-grade
|       cryptography, which is significantly weaker, allowing the attacker
|       to more easily break the encryption and monitor or tamper with
|       the encrypted stream.
